million for letters of credit issued by foreign subsidiaries, subject to the understanding that the outstanding amount of letters of credit issued under the Credit Agreement, combined with the The LC Facility provides for the issuance, at the Lender&#8217;s option and discretion, of letters of credit cash collateralized at 103% of the face amount thereof, in an amount not to exceed (i) $150 million through February 14, 2021 and (ii) $75 million from February 15, 2021 through August 31, 2021.  The Lender may terminate the LC Facility at any time. The Company is obligated to pay a fee of 250 basis points per annum on the daily undrawn face amount of each letter of credit and such additional fees as may be agreed by the Company and the Lender at the time each letter of credit is issued.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify;"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#212529;font-family:'Times New purposes of determining the Alternative Rate if LIBOR is unavailable for any reason.</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Times New
